[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:CelestialBody)

:   "*If I grew up here, I don't think I'd ever leave.*"
:   ―Anakin Skywalker, about Naboo[[21]](#cite_note-AotC-21)

**Naboo** was a bountiful [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") in the [Chommell sector](/wiki/Chommell_sector "Chommell sector") of the [Mid Rim](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories"), in the [Trailing Sectors](/wiki/Trailing_Sectors "Trailing Sectors") and close to the border of the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories"). It was [home](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld") to the indigenous [Gungan](/wiki/Gungan "Gungan") [species](/wiki/Species "Species") and to a population of [humans](/wiki/Human "Human") known as [the Naboo](/wiki/Naboo_(people) "Naboo (people)"). Naboo was pushed to the forefront of [galactic](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") [politics](/wiki/Politics "Politics") as the birthplace of the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), who served as its [representative](/wiki/Naboo_delegation "Naboo delegation") in the [Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate") of the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic").

Under the guise of his [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") title [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious, Palpatine secretly engineered an [invasion](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo") of his peaceful homeworld by the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation"), a [megacorporation](/wiki/Megacorporation "Megacorporation") in a bid for power. Ostensibly done in protest over proposed taxation of formerly free [trade routes](/wiki/Hyperspace_route "Hyperspace route"), the Federation's invasion led to an outpouring of support from the Senate for both Palpatine and the newly-elected [Queen of Naboo](/wiki/Monarch_of_Naboo "Monarch of Naboo"), [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala"). Amidala led a successful [resistance movement](/wiki/Naboo_resistance "Naboo resistance") and removed the Federation from her world during the [Battle of Naboo](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo"). Palpatine subsequently rose to the [office](/wiki/Office_of_the_Chancellor "Office of the Chancellor") of the [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") of the Republic, with Amidala eventually taking his place as the planet's [senatorial](/wiki/Senator "Senator") representative.

Naboo would commit itself firmly to [democracy](/wiki/Democracy "Democracy") in the intervening [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year"), staying loyal to the Republic during the pan-galactic [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), which saw several [military](/wiki/Army "Army") engagements against the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") come to the planet. By the [time](/wiki/Time "Time") of the war's end, Palpatine had amassed considerable power and [proclaimed](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") himself the [head](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") of a new [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"). Palpatine's reign would eventually be [ended](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor") by the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic"), a rebel movement led by Amidala's children, [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo") and [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker").

Despite his origins on the planet, Palpatine did not care at all for his homeworld and, following his [death](/wiki/Death "Death"), Naboo was named a priority target for [Operation: Cinder](/wiki/Operation:_Cinder "Operation: Cinder"), a [protocol](/wiki/Contingency "Contingency") that the Sith Lord had put in place to destroy Imperial worlds should they fail to protect their [Emperor](/wiki/Emperor "Emperor"). Through the [intervention](/wiki/Battle_of_Theed "Battle of Theed") of Organa and [Queen](/wiki/Queen "Queen") [Sosha Soruna](/wiki/Sosha_Soruna "Sosha Soruna"), however, Naboo was spared from ruin and went on to become a member of the successor state to the Alliance, the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic"). [Decades](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade") later, the planet would again fight against tyranny, [rising up](/wiki/Uprising_on_Naboo_(First_Order) "Uprising on Naboo (First Order)") against the military junta of the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order") during its [war](/wiki/First_Order-Resistance_War "First Order-Resistance War") with Organa's [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance").

## Description[]

:   "*It's* beautiful*.*"  
    "*Yes, it absolutely* is.*"*
:   ―Shara Bey and Leia Organa, about Naboo[[54]](#cite_note-ShatteredEmpireII-54)

 [![The picturesque planet of Naboo was located in the galaxy's Mid Rim region.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/24/NabooFull-SW.png/revision/latest?cb=20131223053139) [![The picturesque planet of Naboo was located in the galaxy's Mid Rim region.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/24/NabooFull-SW.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20131223053139)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/24/NabooFull-SW.png/revision/latest?cb=20131223053139) 

The picturesque planet of Naboo was located in the galaxy's Mid Rim region.

 

Naboo was a small pastoral [world](/wiki/Planet "Planet")[[55]](#cite_note-sweSB-55) in the [Mid Rim](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories"),[[1]](#cite_note-Ultimate_SW-1) located near the border of the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories"),[[14]](#cite_note-sweBA-14) 34,000 [light-years](/wiki/Light-year "Light-year") from the [Core Worlds](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds").[[6]](#cite_note-DV1-6) Unlike most other worlds, the ancient planet lacked a molten core, and instead comprised a conglomerate of large, rocky bodies that made up a network of tunnels and flooded caves. The native [Gungans](/wiki/Gungan "Gungan"), who built their homes in the [waters](/wiki/Water "Water") of Naboo, so deep that they went right through the planet, which they rarely ventured into the core, fearing the ravenous sea beasts which resided[[1]](#cite_note-Ultimate_SW-1) in areas such as the [Caves of Eleuabad](/wiki/Caves_of_Eleuabad "Caves of Eleuabad").[[12]](#cite_note-SWCL-12) Despite this, certain Gungan navigators utilized time-honored trade routes through the planet's structure, which served as the most expedient avenues to reach other areas of the planet.[[1]](#cite_note-Ultimate_SW-1) Naboo's interior was rich with [plasma](/wiki/Plasma "Plasma"), a naturally-occurring energy unique to the planet, and this coupled with its lack of molten core gave Naboo a reputation as an enigma to astrophysicists, who regarded the world's structure as an extremely rare phenomenon in [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy").[[12]](#cite_note-SWCL-12)

 [![With its grassy plains and waterfalls, Naboo was known as an idyllic world.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/Attack_of_the_clones_3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160129221934) [![With its grassy plains and waterfalls, Naboo was known as an idyllic world.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/Attack_of_the_clones_3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160129221934)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/Attack_of_the_clones_3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160129221934) 

With its grassy plains and waterfalls, Naboo was known as an idyllic world.

 

Naboo's surface comprised a vast array of different landscapes, from rolling plains and [grassy](/wiki/Grass "Grass") hills to [swampy](/wiki/Swamp "Swamp") lakes[[14]](#cite_note-sweBA-14) caused by the water-filled network of deep-sea tunnels.[[12]](#cite_note-SWCL-12) The swamps acted as a gateway to the world's seas, where legendary creatures dwelt.[[11]](#cite_note-VE-11) Beside its natural features, Naboo was considered a world of classical beauty due to the aesthetics of its population centers.[[14]](#cite_note-sweBA-14) The porous crust's natural plasma[[12]](#cite_note-SWCL-12) was harvested for energy and building material,[[50]](#cite_note-sweGunTech-50) and was generally thought to be the key to many of the planet's secrets.[[12]](#cite_note-SWCL-12)

While most of Naboo's land animals were peaceful, as exemplified by the gentle [shaak](/wiki/Shaak "Shaak"), the planet's [oceans](/wiki/Ocean "Ocean"),[[56]](#cite_note-UFC-56) which held an abundance of life,[[11]](#cite_note-VE-11) teemed with menacing creatures,[[56]](#cite_note-UFC-56) such as the [opee sea killer](/wiki/Opee_sea_killer "Opee sea killer")[[38]](#cite_note-sweOSK-38), the [sando aqua monster](/wiki/Sando_aqua_monster "Sando aqua monster")[[40]](#cite_note-sweSAM-40), and the [colo claw fish](/wiki/Colo_claw_fish "Colo claw fish")[[29]](#cite_note-sweCCF-29).

## History[]

### Early history[]

#### Pre-human colonization[]

 [![Gungans were the original inhabitants of Naboo prior to the arrival of offworlders.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/Nass_on_Sacred_Place.png/revision/latest?cb=20130126035455) [![Gungans were the original inhabitants of Naboo prior to the arrival of offworlders.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/Nass_on_Sacred_Place.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130126035455)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/Nass_on_Sacred_Place.png/revision/latest?cb=20130126035455) 

Gungans were the original inhabitants of Naboo prior to the arrival of offworlders.

 

Originally, Naboo was home to the [amphibian](/wiki/Amphibian "Amphibian") Gungans.[[1]](#cite_note-Ultimate_SW-1) The earliest offworlders to arrive were a [Reptilian](/wiki/Reptile "Reptile") species known as the [Elders](/wiki/Elders_(Naboo) "Elders (Naboo)") who warred against the Gungans. Eventually, the Elders vanished as mysteriously as they arrived, leaving only stone statues behind.[[7]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Separatists-7)

#### Arrival of humanity[]

:   "*Take a moment and look around this glorious city of yours. It wasn't long ago this was all plasma mines. Naboo has indeed come a long way. But as we chart a bold course for the future, let us never forget our past.*"
:   ―Sheev Palpatine[[57]](#cite_note-CoN-57)

 [![The Naboo were the descendants of human colonists who migrated from Grizmallt.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/DeejaPeakFarmers-CrisisOnNaboo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130823011349) [![The Naboo were the descendants of human colonists who migrated from Grizmallt.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/DeejaPeakFarmers-CrisisOnNaboo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20130823011349)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/DeejaPeakFarmers-CrisisOnNaboo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130823011349) 

The Naboo were the descendants of human colonists who migrated from Grizmallt.

 

Approximately around [4000 BBY](/wiki/4,000_BBY "4,000 BBY"), [Grizmallti](/wiki/Grizmallti "Grizmallti") people had discovered the planet, which they had named *Nabu*, after [one of their](/wiki/Nabu "Nabu") principal deities. Naboo quickly became notorious as a vacation spot and as a private hunting preserve amongst big-game hunters across the Mid Rim, although it would be around a century before permanent [human](/wiki/Human "Human") settlement.[[16]](#cite_note-Nexus_of_Power-16) Initially, the Gungans retreated underwater and avoided the colonists[[7]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Separatists-7) and new interlopers.[[16]](#cite_note-Nexus_of_Power-16)

While the Gungans flourished for thousands of years before, this only lasted until around [3900 BBY](/wiki/3900_BBY "3900 BBY"). Fleeing a brutal civil war,[[16]](#cite_note-Nexus_of_Power-16) a group of humans from the planet [Grizmallt](/wiki/Grizmallt "Grizmallt") crash-landed on Naboo and set up a small colony. As they established their own society, they initially kept separate from the Gungans.[[24]](#cite_note-TCVD_NE-24) Led by [Kwilaan](/wiki/Kwilaan "Kwilaan"), the colonists ventured into the [Gallo Mountains](/wiki/Gallo_Mountains "Gallo Mountains"), created a [farming](/wiki/Farm "Farm") community at the [Dee'ja Peak](/wiki/Dee%27ja_Peak "Dee'ja Peak"),[[17]](#cite_note-Crisis-17) establishing their presence on the planet and eventually taking its name for themselves. The [Naboo calendar](/wiki/Naboo_calendar "Naboo calendar") based its epoch around the arrival of Kwilaan.[[58]](#cite_note-SWP-58) When the colonists made contact with the Gungans, tensions arose between the two peoples, culminating a [series of wars](/wiki/Human-Gungan_conflicts "Human-Gungan conflicts") between the two species.[[7]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Separatists-7) They subsequently resolved to separate and live apart from that point on.[[59]](#cite_note-sweBN-59)

The Naboo colonists later expanded to other uninhabited planets in the [Chommell sector](/wiki/Chommell_sector "Chommell sector"), such as [Karlinus](/wiki/Karlinus "Karlinus"). Naboo imposed a contract on the colonists of these other planets, wherein Naboo would give the new colonies a loan to cover the start-up costs of colonization. In exchange, the colonies became legally obligated to provide Naboo with any supplies it deemed were necessary if called upon in times of emergency. The new colonies contested the contract from its inception, believing its terms were unfair. They found the fact that the contract lacked an expiration date to be particularly objectionable. Under the contract, Naboo took advantage of every other planet in the Chommell sector from time to time.[[60]](#cite_note-Queen's_Hope-60)

#### Gungan tribal war[]

:   "*Gungans no dyin' witout a fight. Wesa warriors.*"
:   ―Jar Jar Binks[[13]](#cite_note-TPM-13)

 [![The Gungans built their underwater capital of Otoh Gunga following a tribal war.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/54/Gungan_society.png/revision/latest?cb=20140421172140) [![The Gungans built their underwater capital of Otoh Gunga following a tribal war.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/54/Gungan_society.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140421172140)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/54/Gungan_society.png/revision/latest?cb=20140421172140) 

The Gungans built their underwater capital of Otoh Gunga following a tribal war.

 

Following the wars with humans, the Gungan tribes engaged in [war](/wiki/Gungan_tribal_war "Gungan tribal war") with each other. The war came to an end due to the actions of [Boss](/wiki/Boss "Boss") [Gallo](/wiki/Gallo "Gallo"), a Gungan who united the tribes under one banner through diplomatic and military means. Gallo eventually [attacked](/wiki/Destruction_of_Spearhead "Destruction of Spearhead") the [city](/wiki/City "City") [Spearhead](/wiki/Spearhead "Spearhead"), which was the home of the rogue [warlord](/wiki/Warlord "Warlord") Boss [Rogoe](/wiki/Rogoe "Rogoe") and the other Gungan holdouts, with a massive Gungan [army](/wiki/Gallo%27s_army "Gallo's army"). Gallo then founded the Gungan capital [Otoh Gunga](/wiki/Otoh_Gunga "Otoh Gunga") on Spearhead's foundations.[[16]](#cite_note-Nexus_of_Power-16)

#### Times of Suffering and Peace[]

##### Struggles give way to peace[]

:   "*It is an honor to be here for this momentous occasion. The pride I feel for this planet cannot be put into words. 847 years ago, Naboo joined the Republic. And tonight. we celebrate that union.*"
:   ―Sheev Palpatine[[57]](#cite_note-CoN-57)

 [![The Naboo had achieved a state of peace and prosperity at the end of a prolonged period of brutal conflict.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/Naboo2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111001152535) [![The Naboo had achieved a state of peace and prosperity at the end of a prolonged period of brutal conflict.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/Naboo2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111001152535)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/Naboo2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111001152535) 

The Naboo had achieved a state of peace and prosperity at the end of a prolonged period of brutal conflict.

 

Meanwhile, the [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo_(people) "Naboo (people)") had fallen prey to a [long period of brutal infighting](/wiki/Time_of_Suffering "Time of Suffering") among the large [city-states](/wiki/City-state "City-state") of humans that inhabited the planet. Eventually, a [general](/wiki/General "General") named [Jafan](/wiki/Jafan "Jafan") managed to end the war, uniting the opposing factions through both force of arms and force of will.[[16]](#cite_note-Nexus_of_Power-16) He became [King](/wiki/King "King") Jafan, [ruler](/wiki/Monarch_of_Naboo "Monarch of Naboo") of all the Naboo,[[12]](#cite_note-SWCL-12) and ushered in the [Great Time of Peace](/wiki/Great_Time_of_Peace "Great Time of Peace").[[16]](#cite_note-Nexus_of_Power-16)

In [867 BBY](/wiki/867_BBY "867 BBY"), Naboo joined the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"),[[61]](#cite_note-Crisis_date-61) the [democratic](/wiki/Democracy "Democracy") union that sought to govern the [galaxy](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy").[[62]](#cite_note-sweGR-62) The people of Naboo celebrated this event during the [Festival of Light](/wiki/Festival_of_Light "Festival of Light").[[57]](#cite_note-CoN-57) In [832 BBY](/wiki/832_BBY "832 BBY"), under the direction of King Jafan, the [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") city of [Theed](/wiki/Theed "Theed") was founded along the banks of the [Solleu River](/wiki/Solleu_River "Solleu River") with the [Theed Royal Palace](/wiki/Theed_Royal_Palace "Theed Royal Palace") built on the [Cliffs of Theed](/wiki/Cliffs_of_Theed "Cliffs of Theed").[[16]](#cite_note-Nexus_of_Power-16)

##### High Republic Era[]

In [382 BBY](/wiki/382_BBY "382 BBY")[[63]](#cite_note-383_Date-63) during the [High Republic Era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era"), Naboo was under the rule of a [queen](/wiki/Unidentified_Queen_of_Naboo_(382_BBY) "Unidentified Queen of Naboo (382 BBY)"), from whom [Axel Greylark](/wiki/Axel_Greylark "Axel Greylark"), a [gambler](/wiki/Gambler "Gambler") and son of [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Kyong Greylark](/wiki/Kyong_Greylark "Kyong Greylark"), wanted to buy a [yacht](/wiki/Unidentified_Queen_of_Naboo%27s_yacht "Unidentified Queen of Naboo's yacht"). At the same time, fellow Supreme Chancellor [Orlen Mollo](/wiki/Orlen_Mollo "Orlen Mollo") traveled across the [Galactic Frontier](/wiki/Galactic_Frontier "Galactic Frontier") aboard the *[Paxion](/wiki/Paxion "Paxion")*, which displayed different vistas from various currently-distant worlds on a wall of its library. During a mission to end the [Eiram and E'ronoh War](/wiki/Eiram_and_E%27ronoh_War "Eiram and E'ronoh War"), it displayed the [Theed Royal Palace](/wiki/Theed_Royal_Palace "Theed Royal Palace") and other sites. The Naboo Palace and the city of [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant") were the only locations [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Gella Nattai](/wiki/Gella_Nattai "Gella Nattai") recognized. Asked to attend along with delegates from numerous other worlds by Chancellors Mollo and Greylark, delegates from Naboo, wearing their cultural clothing, arrived on [Eiram](/wiki/Eiram "Eiram") for the [wedding of Phan-tu Zenn and Xiri A'lbaran](/wiki/Wedding_of_Phan-tu_Zenn_and_Xiri_A%27lbaran "Wedding of Phan-tu Zenn and Xiri A'lbaran") that promised to end the war. At least two Gungans attended the celebration.[[64]](#cite_note-Convergence-64)

Later in the High Republic Era, the former [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") [Kantam Sy](/wiki/Kantam_Sy "Kantam Sy") found the [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") [Lula Talisola](/wiki/Lula_Mrala-Talisola "Lula Mrala-Talisola") amongst the [children](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling") cared for at an [orphanage](/wiki/Unidentified_orphanage_(Naboo) "Unidentified orphanage (Naboo)") on Naboo. Returning to the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"), Sy became a [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") and Talisola's master.[[65]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-65) A [Jedi temple](/wiki/Jedi_temple "Jedi temple") on Naboo, the [Gallo Temple](/wiki/Gallo_Temple "Gallo Temple"), was also established at some point and regarded as a much-prized posting for [Jedi Knights](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight"). It was the first posting of [Elzar Mann](/wiki/Elzar_Mann "Elzar Mann") after being knighted.[[66]](#cite_note-The_High_Republic:_The_Rising_Storm-66) By 232 BBY,[[67]](#cite_note-Timelines-67) the scion of the wealthy [San Tekka clan](/wiki/San_Tekka_clan "San Tekka clan"), [Vellis](/wiki/Vellis_San_Tekka "Vellis San Tekka"), was based on Naboo, alongside his husband, [Marlowe](/wiki/Marlowe_San_Tekka "Marlowe San Tekka"), living in a large estate by the [lakes](/wiki/Lake_Country "Lake Country").[[25]](#cite_note-LotJ-25)

##### Reign of the Nihil[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main articles: [Occupation of Naboo](/wiki/Occupation_of_Naboo "Occupation of Naboo") and [Second occupation of Naboo](/wiki/Second_occupation_of_Naboo "Second occupation of Naboo")

In [228 BBY](/wiki/228_BBY "228 BBY"),[[68]](#cite_note-228_Date-68) with the creation of the [Stormwall](/wiki/Stormwall "Stormwall") by the [Nihil](/wiki/Nihil "Nihil") and its subsequent expansions, Naboo was eventually included in the [Occlusion Zone](/wiki/Occlusion_Zone "Occlusion Zone"). The Nihil General [Abediah Viess](/wiki/Abediah_Viess "Abediah Viess") led an [invasion of Naboo](/wiki/Takeover_of_Naboo "Takeover of Naboo"), establishing the planet as a military base and putting it under [Nihil occupation](/wiki/Occupation_of_Naboo "Occupation of Naboo"). [Theed](/wiki/Theed "Theed") was conquered after a barrage of Nihil [ion blasts](/wiki/Ion_cannon "Ion cannon") took out the capital's [plasma](/wiki/Plasma "Plasma") mine shafts, creating a planet-wide blackout. Without energy, two-thirds of the [Royal Space Fighter Corps](/wiki/Naboo_Royal_Space_Fighter_Corps "Naboo Royal Space Fighter Corps") were left inactive, facilitating the Nihil takeover of the planet. The [gungans](/wiki/Gungan "Gungan") remained retrated in their underwater cities, and the [reigning queen](/wiki/Unidentified_Queen_of_Naboo_(228_BBY) "Unidentified Queen of Naboo (228 BBY)") managed to escape into hiding with help from the [Royal Security Forces](/wiki/Royal_Naboo_Security_Forces "Royal Naboo Security Forces").[[69]](#cite_note-:0-69)

Under the supervision of Viess, the Nihil occupation of the planet enacted a widespread forced disarmament, and subsequently took a considerable amount of resources from the richer inhabitants of Naboo as "tribute". Although the quick Nihil victory meant that the occupation on Naboo was less ruthless on the general population than the ones on other planets inside the Occlusion Zone, the initial raid led to some amount of casualties. A joint Jedi-[Republic Defense Coalition](/wiki/Republic_Defense_Coalition "Republic Defense Coalition") [assault on Naboo](/wiki/Assault_on_Naboo "Assault on Naboo") was later able to liberate the world.[[69]](#cite_note-:0-69)

##### Late High Republic Era[]

By [132 BBY](/wiki/132_BBY "132 BBY")[[70]](#cite_note-132Date-70) and as the light of the High Republic had begun to fade,[[71]](#cite_note-Launchpad_231-71) Naboo and the rest of the Chommel sector were represented in the Galactic Senate of the Republic by Senator [Sahen Idane](/wiki/Sahen_Idane "Sahen Idane"), a longtime ally of the Jedi Order and also someone who enjoyed close ties with Naboo royalty. Queen [Yovité](/wiki/Yovit%C3%A9 "Yovité"), who by that time had been elected Queen, had gifted a belt sash to Yovité by that year. Yovité also donned fabric sourced from a refinery in Theed.[[72]](#cite_note-Acolyte_Visual_Guide-72)

### Twilight of the Republic[]

#### Invasion of Naboo[]

:   "*I was not elected to watch my people suffer and die while you discuss this invasion in a committee.*"
:   ―Queen Amidala, to the Galactic Senate — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/11/IWasNotElected-TPM.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250407192715)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:IWasNotElected-TPM.flac "File:IWasNotElected-TPM.flac"))[[13]](#cite_note-TPM-13)

The fourteen year old [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala") was elected to be the new Monarch of Naboo after Queen [Sanandrassa](/wiki/Sanandrassa "Sanandrassa") decided to only have a single term. While Sanandrassa favored isolationism, Amidala wanted to promote friendship with other planets in the Chommell sector, leading to her hosting the [Chommell sector summit](/wiki/Chommell_sector_summit "Chommell sector summit"). Additionally, after being urged to by [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Quarsh Panaka](/wiki/Quarsh_Panaka "Quarsh Panaka"), Amidala took on a group of [Handmaidens](/wiki/Handmaiden "Handmaiden"), whom she quickly befriended, planning her days with them instead of Panaka.[[48]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-48)

 [![The capital of Theed fell to the forces of the Trade Federation during the Invasion of Naboo.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/TheedAttack.png/revision/latest?cb=20120927141009) [![The capital of Theed fell to the forces of the Trade Federation during the Invasion of Naboo.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/TheedAttack.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120927141009)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/TheedAttack.png/revision/latest?cb=20120927141009) 

The capital of Theed fell to the forces of the Trade Federation during the Invasion of Naboo.

 

Right as the Naboo summit ended,[[48]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-48) about ten [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), Naboo was [blockaded](/wiki/Blockade "Blockade") and [invaded](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo") by the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation"). Amidala guided her [home planet](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld") through the invasion and sealed a new [friendship](/wiki/Boss_Meetup "Boss Meetup") with the Gungans.[[73]](#cite_note-swePA-73) In an upsurge of sympathy and solidarity toward the invaded planet, the [queen](/wiki/Queen "Queen")'s emissary in the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate"), the seemingly unassuming [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), was made [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") of the Republic.[[13]](#cite_note-TPM-13)

Naboo recovered quickly from the invasion under Amidala's remaining years, managing to almost completely restore its harvests and crop yields by the end of her final term. One of Amidala's final projects, which continued under the reign of her successor, was the implementation of an ion pulse in Theed in case of future invasions. The decision to install the pulse, whilst meeting with general approval, was nevertheless controversial as some, such as Quarsh Panaka, favored the idea of more robust and extensive defenses whilst others felt that installing any weapon system was against everything Naboo stood for in terms of peace.[[74]](#cite_note-Queen's_Shadow-74)

#### Clone Wars[]

:   "*I need you to convince the Senate, or the Jedi Council, or whoever is in charge of this terrible war that we are threatened.*"
:   ―Neeyutnee, to Padmé Amidala[[27]](#cite_note-Blue_Shadow_Virus-27)

 [![The government of Naboo remained loyal to the Galactic Republic during the Separatist Crisis and the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/75/Naboo_Throne_Room.png/revision/latest?cb=20130720034408) [![The government of Naboo remained loyal to the Galactic Republic during the Separatist Crisis and the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/75/Naboo_Throne_Room.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130720034408)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/75/Naboo_Throne_Room.png/revision/latest?cb=20130720034408) 

The government of Naboo remained loyal to the Galactic Republic during the Separatist Crisis and the Clone Wars.

 

A [series of miners strikes](/wiki/Naboo_miners%27_strikes "Naboo miners' strikes") occurred on the moons of Naboo.[[10]](#cite_note-Leia-10) A [mudslide disaster](/wiki/Mudslide_disaster "Mudslide disaster") occurred on Naboo's secondary continent[[60]](#cite_note-Queen's_Hope-60) in [22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY").[[75]](#cite_note-Hope_Date-75) Both the Naboo and the Gungans remained loyal to the Republic during the Clone Wars, though many on Naboo were in despair at the idea of a galaxy-wide war. Senator Padmé Amidala and [Representative](/wiki/Junior_Representative "Junior Representative") [Jar Jar Binks](/wiki/Jar_Jar_Binks "Jar Jar Binks") worked together to represent the interests of the Naboo and Gungans respectively in the Galactic Senate.[[21]](#cite_note-AotC-21) During the Clone Wars, [Neeyutnee](/wiki/Neeyutnee "Neeyutnee") served as Queen of Naboo.[[27]](#cite_note-Blue_Shadow_Virus-27) Early in the war, Amidala and Skywalker returned to the planet for their [wedding](/wiki/Wedding_of_Anakin_Skywalker_and_Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Wedding of Anakin Skywalker and Padmé Amidala")[[21]](#cite_note-AotC-21) and spent several days on world for a honeymoon.[[60]](#cite_note-Queen's_Hope-60)

When a number of new battles, including the [Battle of Teth](/wiki/Battle_of_Teth "Battle of Teth"), rocked the Outer Rim Territories[[76]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-76) a few months into the war,[[77]](#cite_note-Boba_Fett_and_Other_Bounty_Hunters_and_Criminals-77) Naboo was put under the protection of several new security measures at the order of Palpatine himself. Amidala wanted to discuss those measures with the Chancellor before learning of the Battle of Teth, which had endangered Skywalker's life and changed her priorities to focusing on the [Hutt–Republic treaty](/wiki/Hutt%E2%80%93Republic_treaty "Hutt–Republic treaty").[[76]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-76) Amidala and Binks, with the help of the Jedi Order and the Gungan [Peppi Bow](/wiki/Peppi_Bow "Peppi Bow"), discovered the [Separatist](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") [scientist](/wiki/Scientist "Scientist") [Nuvo Vindi](/wiki/Nuvo_Vindi "Nuvo Vindi")'s [secret laboratory](/wiki/Trade_Federation_laboratory "Trade Federation laboratory") in the [Eastern swamps](/wiki/Eastern_swamps "Eastern swamps").[[27]](#cite_note-Blue_Shadow_Virus-27) They managed to prevent Vindi from releasing stockpiles of the [Blue Shadow Virus](/wiki/Blue_Shadow_Virus "Blue Shadow Virus") into Naboo's surface.[[78]](#cite_note-Mystery_of_a_Thousand_Moons-78) During the [Battle of Mon Cala](/wiki/Battle_of_Mon_Cala "Battle of Mon Cala"), elements of the [Gungan Grand Army](/wiki/Gungan_Grand_Army "Gungan Grand Army") led by Representative Binks were dispatched to the watery planet of [Mon Cala](/wiki/Mon_Cala "Mon Cala") to aid Senator Amidala, the Jedi, the [Clone SCUBA troopers](/wiki/Clone_SCUBA_trooper "Clone SCUBA trooper"), and the [Mon Calamari](/wiki/Mon_Calamari "Mon Calamari") [Prince](/wiki/Prince "Prince") [Lee-Char](/wiki/Lee-Char "Lee-Char")'s forces against the Separatist [commander](/wiki/Commander "Commander") [Riff Tamson](/wiki/Riff_Tamson "Riff Tamson") and his [Quarren](/wiki/Quarren "Quarren") allies.[[79]](#cite_note-Gungan_Attack-79)

 [![By working together the Naboo and the Gungans prevented a Separatist attack on their shared homeworld.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/NeeyutneeLeaves-SW.png/revision/latest?cb=20121122163024) [![By working together the Naboo and the Gungans prevented a Separatist attack on their shared homeworld.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/NeeyutneeLeaves-SW.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121122163024)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/NeeyutneeLeaves-SW.png/revision/latest?cb=20121122163024) 

By working together the Naboo and the Gungans prevented a Separatist attack on their shared homeworld.

 

Later, the Gungan Boss [Lyonie](/wiki/Lyonie "Lyonie") came under the influence of the pro-Separatist [minister](/wiki/Minister "Minister") [Rish Loo](/wiki/Rish_Loo "Rish Loo"). Under Loo's control, Lyonie ordered the Gungan Grand Army to march on the Naboo capital of Theed. Their plan was to rendezvous with a Separatist [droid](/wiki/Droid "Droid") [army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army") led by General [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous"), who had been sent by [Count](/wiki/Count "Count") [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku") himself. Rish Loo and Dooku's [plot](/wiki/Skirmish_on_Naboo "Skirmish on Naboo") was foiled by the combined efforts of Senator Amidala, Representative Binks, the Jedi Knight [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), and General [Roos Tarpals](/wiki/Roos_Tarpals "Roos Tarpals"). However, the Naboo and Gungans were forced to release Grievous after Dooku took Skywalker hostage.[[23]](#cite_note-Shadow_Warrior-23)

During the Festival of Light, Dooku sent [Cad Bane](/wiki/Cad_Bane "Cad Bane") and his team of [bounty hunters](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") to [kidnap](/wiki/Plan_to_kidnap_Chancellor_Palpatine "Plan to kidnap Chancellor Palpatine") Palpatine in order to free Separatist [prisoners](/wiki/Prisoner "Prisoner") from Republic captivity. At first, Bane and [Moralo Eval](/wiki/Moralo_Eval "Moralo Eval") were successful in capturing Palpatine. However, they were stopped by one of their fellow bounty hunters, [Rako Hardeen](/wiki/Rako_Hardeen "Rako Hardeen"), who was really [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") in disguise. But, Bane planned a diversion in order to lure the Republic forces away while Dooku carried out the kidnapping. This failed, however, when he fought Kenobi and Skywalker.[[57]](#cite_note-CoN-57)

### The dark times[]

:   "*Palpatine's* stain *is heavy on our people, and we carry that shame* still*.*"
:   ―Sosha Soruna[[54]](#cite_note-ShatteredEmpireII-54)

 [![Naboo was in a state of mourning for Padmé Amidala, who died following the rise of the Galactic Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/Frontfuneral.png/revision/latest?cb=20130206005622) [![Naboo was in a state of mourning for Padmé Amidala, who died following the rise of the Galactic Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/Frontfuneral.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130206005622)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/Frontfuneral.png/revision/latest?cb=20130206005622) 

Naboo was in a state of mourning for Padmé Amidala, who died following the rise of the Galactic Empire.

 

Following the rise of the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") and Palpatine's [self-proclamation](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") as [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor"), Naboo hosted one of the new regime's military garrisons.[[51]](#cite_note-BS-51) Shortly after the end of the Clone Wars, thousands of citizens gathered in the streets of Theed in order to assist to Amidala's [funeral procession](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala%27s_funeral "Padmé Amidala's funeral").[[80]](#cite_note-Episode_III-80) At that time, Sio Bibble had finally decided to retire from governorship over Naboo, setting the stage for an election that [Saché](/wiki/Sach%C3%A9 "Saché") was seemingly going to win.[[74]](#cite_note-Queen's_Shadow-74) However, Naboo's internal politics were also interfered with by the new regime; while the people were still permitted to elect their monarchs, those who gained the office had little real power or influence.[[81]](#cite_note-Leia_of_Alderaan-81) The position of governor was also abolished.[[74]](#cite_note-Queen's_Shadow-74) Instead, all major decisions regarding Naboo were placed firmly in the hands of the sector's [Moff](/wiki/Moff "Moff"), a position held by[[81]](#cite_note-Leia_of_Alderaan-81) Palpatine's close ally[[48]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-48) and former Security Forces [officer](/wiki/Officer "Officer") Quarsh Panaka,[[81]](#cite_note-Leia_of_Alderaan-81) who was appointed before the election for governor could even happen.[[74]](#cite_note-Queen's_Shadow-74)

Some time around [18 BBY](/wiki/18_BBY "18 BBY"), [Luthen Rael](/wiki/Luthen_Rael "Luthen Rael") and his adoptive daughter [Kleya Marki](/wiki/Kleya_Marki "Kleya Marki") [bombed](/wiki/Bombing_on_Naboo "Bombing on Naboo") [Imperial vehicles](/wiki/Unidentified_troop_transport "Unidentified troop transport") on a Nabooian bridge as an early act of their rebellion.[[82]](#cite_note-Stop-82)

 [![Darth Vader on Naboo in 3 ABY](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/VaderStandsOnNaboo-2020DarthVader3.png/revision/latest?cb=20231113123404) [![Darth Vader on Naboo in 3 ABY](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/VaderStandsOnNaboo-2020DarthVader3.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20231113123404)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/VaderStandsOnNaboo-2020DarthVader3.png/revision/latest?cb=20231113123404) 

Darth Vader on Naboo in 3 ABY

 

Though one of the less corrupt Imperial officials, Panaka was [assassinated](/wiki/Strike_on_Onoam "Strike on Onoam") by [Saw Gerrera](/wiki/Saw_Gerrera "Saw Gerrera")'s [Partisans](/wiki/Partisans "Partisans") insurgency[[81]](#cite_note-Leia_of_Alderaan-81) in [3 BBY](/wiki/3_BBY "3 BBY").[[67]](#cite_note-Timelines-67) Due to its status as Palpatine's homeworld, Naboo prospered during the [Age of the Empire](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"). Its economy and environment were regarded to be far healthier than most worlds which had been subject to Imperial rule.[[52]](#cite_note-Lost_Stars-52) Nevertheless, the people of Naboo resented the fact that it was their world that brought forth a man like Palpatine. The Empire also demilitarized Naboo and dissolved the [Royal Naboo Security Forces](/wiki/Royal_Naboo_Security_Forces "Royal Naboo Security Forces")'s [starfighter](/wiki/N-1_starfighter "N-1 starfighter") wing. As a result, Naboo lacked any combat-trained [pilots](/wiki/Pilot "Pilot") by the [time](/wiki/Time "Time") of the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor").[[83]](#cite_note-ShatteredEmpireIII-83)

[Sabé](/wiki/Sab%C3%A9 "Sabé"), former handmaiden of Padme Amidala, brought Darth Vader to Naboo in [3 ABY](/wiki/3_ABY "3 ABY"). [Typho](/wiki/Gregar_Typho "Gregar Typho") and his rebel team fought him. The rebels went as far as baiting a Sando aqua monster into fighting the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith"). [Ric Olié](/wiki/Ric_Oli%C3%A9 "Ric Olié") and his rebel cell, [the Amidalans](/wiki/Amidalans "Amidalans"), attempted to protect Padmé's tomb from Vader, but were killed in the process. The handmaidens gathered for a final stand. They were unable to prevent Darth Vader from breaching the tomb.[[84]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_4-84)

### A new era[]

#### Rise of the New Republic[]

:   "*…Very simply this, that Naboo represents the* best *of the Old Republic. Its assistance—*your *assistance, Your Highness—would be* invaluable *in leading the way to a restoration of the* Senate*. As we attempt to form a* new *government, we hope we may rely on Naboo's support, counsel, and aid.*"
:   ―Leia Organa, to Sosha Soruna[[54]](#cite_note-ShatteredEmpireII-54)

 [![The death of Galactic Emperor Sheev Palpatine was celebrated on his homeworld of Naboo by humans and Gungans alike.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/Theed.png/revision/latest?cb=20130422013922) [![The death of Galactic Emperor Sheev Palpatine was celebrated on his homeworld of Naboo by humans and Gungans alike.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/Theed.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130422013922)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/Theed.png/revision/latest?cb=20130422013922) 

The death of Galactic Emperor Sheev Palpatine was celebrated on his homeworld of Naboo by humans and Gungans alike.

 

When news of Emperor Palpatine's [death](/wiki/Death "Death") during the Battle of Endor—which resulted in[[85]](#cite_note-ROJ-85) the apparent[[86]](#cite_note-TPATS-86) defeat of the Empire by the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic")—spread across the galaxy after the battle, an outpouring of joy [occurred](/wiki/Rally_on_Naboo "Rally on Naboo") on Naboo, the inhabitants of which considered themselves free at last.[[85]](#cite_note-ROJ-85) While it quickly became apparent that the war was not over as the Empire survived, even without its Emperor,[[86]](#cite_note-TPATS-86) Naboo was liberated from Imperial control. Nonetheless, all equipment stored within Palpatine's small countryside retreat was stripped bare by the time it was explored by the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic"), preventing the government from discovering whatever secrets Palpatine had kept within.[[87]](#cite_note-Rise_and_Fall-87)

Some twenty [days](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day") after the Battle of Endor, the [Royal House of Naboo](/wiki/Royal_House_of_Naboo "Royal House of Naboo") received a visit by Princess [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo") of [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan"), who had been sent by [Mon Mothma](/wiki/Mon_Mothma "Mon Mothma"), [Chancellor](/wiki/Chancellor_(Rebel_Alliance) "Chancellor (Rebel Alliance)") of the Alliance,[[54]](#cite_note-ShatteredEmpireII-54) which was in the process of reorganizing into the New Republic.[[88]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-88)[[86]](#cite_note-TPATS-86) In the royal palace's throne room, Organa met the then-Queen of Naboo, [Sosha Soruna](/wiki/Sosha_Soruna "Sosha Soruna"), and asked for Naboo's support in the establishment of the New Republic and the restoration of the [Senate](/wiki/New_Republic_Senate "New Republic Senate"). The queen heartily accepted Organa's offer, claiming that the Naboo felt great shame over Palpatine's actions.[[54]](#cite_note-ShatteredEmpireII-54)

#### Operation: Cinder[]

:   "*Jamming at full power, Captain. Climate disruption array now at twenty percent. We count* three *class-five hurricanes already, another dozen* forming*.*"  
    "*I want one hundred percent within eight hours, Lieutenant Gulin. By order of the Emperor…Naboo is to be* scoured*…*"
:   ―[Gulin](/wiki/Gulin "Gulin") and [Lerr Duvat](/wiki/Lerr_Duvat "Lerr Duvat")[[54]](#cite_note-ShatteredEmpireII-54)

 [![Aided by the Rebel Alliance, the Naboo fought to save their world from the Empire during Operation: Cinder.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/SWBF2_Battle_of_Naboo_Space.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20171115190326) [![Aided by the Rebel Alliance, the Naboo fought to save their world from the Empire during Operation: Cinder.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/SWBF2_Battle_of_Naboo_Space.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20171115190326)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/SWBF2_Battle_of_Naboo_Space.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20171115190326) 

Aided by the Rebel Alliance, the Naboo fought to save their world from the Empire during Operation: Cinder.

 

During the meeting, gigantic storms suddenly began to rage, and Naboo's orbital [sensors](/wiki/Sensor "Sensor") were all jammed. The Empire had set up a [climate disruption array](/wiki/Climate_disruption_array "Climate disruption array") in [orbit](/wiki/Orbit "Orbit"), as ordered by the late Emperor Palpatine. Named [Operation: Cinder](/wiki/Operation:_Cinder "Operation: Cinder"), the Empire's plan was to disrupt Naboo's environment and climate, and thus render the planet inhospitable.[[54]](#cite_note-ShatteredEmpireII-54) The storms caused [fires](/wiki/Fire "Fire") and flooding across the world, and many buildings were demolished. Soruna, Organa, and Alliance pilot [Shara Bey](/wiki/Shara_Bey "Shara Bey") finally decided to use three old N-1 [starfighters](/wiki/Starfighter "Starfighter")—that had been stored by Queen Neeyutnee in the [Theed Hangar](/wiki/Theed_Hangar "Theed Hangar") during the Clone Wars—and go protect Naboo by [destroying](/wiki/Battle_of_Theed "Battle of Theed") the Empire's [satellites](/wiki/Satellite "Satellite"). Once in [space](/wiki/Realspace "Realspace"), the three [women](/wiki/Gender "Gender") were attacked by a [squadron](/wiki/Squadron "Squadron") of [TIE fighters](/wiki/TIE/ln_space_superiority_starfighter "TIE/ln space superiority starfighter"), but managed, nonetheless, to knock out all of the satellites. A [Rebel fleet](/wiki/Rebel_Alliance_Navy "Rebel Alliance Navy") led by [Lando Calrissian](/wiki/Landonis_Balthazar_Calrissian "Landonis Balthazar Calrissian") and [Nien Nunb](/wiki/Nien_Nunb "Nien Nunb") soon arrived to take care of the Imperial forces.[[83]](#cite_note-ShatteredEmpireIII-83) The fleet consisted of members of [Danger Squadron](/wiki/Danger_Squadron "Danger Squadron"), which arrived in [T-65B X-wing starfighters](/wiki/T-65B_X-wing_starfighter "T-65B X-wing starfighter") led by [Danger Leader](/wiki/Danger_Leader "Danger Leader") [Duros](/wiki/Duros "Duros") [Shriv Suurgav](/wiki/Shriv_Suurgav "Shriv Suurgav"),[[88]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-88) Nunb in the *[Mellcrawler II](/wiki/Mellcrawler_II "Mellcrawler II")*, and the [MC80 Star Cruiser](/wiki/MC80_Star_Cruiser "MC80 Star Cruiser") *[Restoration](/wiki/Restoration "Restoration")*.[[83]](#cite_note-ShatteredEmpireIII-83)

 [![With their weapons and vehicles disabled by Theed's ion defense, the Imperials were forced to surrender to the Naboo and their Rebel allies.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/NabooIonPulse.png/revision/latest?cb=20171123205226) [![With their weapons and vehicles disabled by Theed's ion defense, the Imperials were forced to surrender to the Naboo and their Rebel allies.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/NabooIonPulse.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20171123205226)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/NabooIonPulse.png/revision/latest?cb=20171123205226) 

With their weapons and vehicles disabled by Theed's ion defense, the Imperials were forced to surrender to the Naboo and their Rebel allies.

 

Danger Squadron temporarily included former [Inferno Squad](/wiki/Inferno_Squad "Inferno Squad") members and recent Imperial defectors [Iden Versio](/wiki/Iden_Versio "Iden Versio") and [Del Meeko](/wiki/Del_Meeko "Del Meeko") to assist the three women in the destruction of the satellites. After their destruction, the [*Imperial II*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Imperial_II-class_Star_Destroyer "Imperial II-class Star Destroyer") *[Torment](/wiki/Torment "Torment")* was then engaged by Danger Squadron and several [Y-wing bombers](/wiki/BTL-A4_Y-wing_assault_starfighter/bomber "BTL-A4 Y-wing assault starfighter/bomber"), and the *Restoration* delivered the fatal blow to the hull of the *Torment*. The Alliance forces then gathered upon the ground to immobilize remaining Imperials in the final ground assault to try and take control of Theed. Imperial forces were immobilized by the [ion pulse](/wiki/Ion_pulse "Ion pulse") courtesy of Leia, Del, Shriv and Iden taking the fight from the marketplace, courtyard and all the way to the palace and once they are inside the pulse activates and rendering all of their weapons and vehicles inoperable leading to the surrender of Imperial forces. And Shriv commented that they just won and after all that happened Iden and Del are formally welcomed by Leia into the New Republic.[[88]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-88)

Due to the fact that Naboo had been the Emperor's homeworld, the planet became a rallying point for Imperial sympathizers. [Months](/wiki/Standard_month "Standard month") after the failed Operation: Cinder, the [Imperial Navy](/wiki/Imperial_Navy "Imperial Navy") deployed three [attack forces](/wiki/Invasions_of_Naboo "Invasions of Naboo") to wipe out the New Republic's presence in the [Naboo system](/wiki/Naboo_system "Naboo system"). However, these attempts were successfully foiled by [Corona Squadron](/wiki/Corona_Squadron "Corona Squadron").[[52]](#cite_note-Lost_Stars-52)

### Rise of the First Order[]

:   "*People of Naboo. This is the Supreme Leader of the First Order. I have commandeered your communications network. I am unimpressed with you. Your focus on events that happened decades ago, your obsession with lineage and superstition…have caused your society to fester. Because you cannot let go…you hold yourself back. Now that will change. All that was will be swept away. Naboo will embrace the future. You have been ruled by queens. You have been ruled by an emperor. Now…I am your king.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren[[89]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_4-89)

During the [Cold War](/wiki/Cold_War "Cold War") nearly thirty years later between the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order") and the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance"), Senator [Thadlé Berenko](/wiki/Thadl%C3%A9_Berenko "Thadlé Berenko") represented Naboo in the reconstituted New Republic Senate,[[90]](#cite_note-TVD-90) and was [killed](/wiki/Death "Death") when the First Order [destroyed](/wiki/Hosnian_Cataclysm "Hosnian Cataclysm") [Hosnian Prime](/wiki/Hosnian_Prime "Hosnian Prime"), the home of the Senate at the time.[[91]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-91)

By [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY"),[[92]](#cite_note-Date-92) Naboo's skies were being patrolled by Star Destroyers from the First Order as part of its expansive efforts to establish galactic dominance. At some point later, Naboo engaged in [open rebellion](/wiki/Uprising_against_the_First_Order "Uprising against the First Order") [against](/wiki/Uprising_on_Naboo_(First_Order) "Uprising on Naboo (First Order)") the First Order, simultaneous with other planets such as [Bespin](/wiki/Uprising_on_Cloud_City "Uprising on Cloud City") and [Coruscant](/wiki/Uprising_on_Coruscant "Uprising on Coruscant") leading to the successful overthrow of the entire regime.[[93]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-93)

## Society and culture[]

:   "*You and the Naboo form a symbiont circle. What happens to one of you will affect the other. You must understand this.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to [Rugor Nass](/wiki/Rugor_Nass "Rugor Nass")[[13]](#cite_note-TPM-13)

 [![The commitment to the defense of Naboo brought its human and Gungan inhabitants together when threatened by an external enemy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/Naboo_celebration.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111008202536) [![The commitment to the defense of Naboo brought its human and Gungan inhabitants together when threatened by an external enemy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/Naboo_celebration.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111008202536)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/Naboo_celebration.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111008202536) 

The commitment to the defense of Naboo brought its human and Gungan inhabitants together when threatened by an external enemy.

 

Naboo was inhabited by two societies: an indigenous species of intelligent amphibians called the Gungans and a group of peaceful humans who were referred to as the Naboo.[[14]](#cite_note-sweBA-14) In the distant past, a cultural misunderstanding resulted in a serious quarrel between the Gungan and the human colonists. Both sides refused to acknowledge their responsibilities in the rift, and the two groups ostracized each other for the longest time. That situation lasted until the Invasion of Naboo by the Trade Federation forced the humans and Gungans to join forces.[[59]](#cite_note-sweBN-59)

Naboo culture fostered the artist in every citizen, encouraging children to become musicians, performers, painters, and similar professions. There were several schools on the planet where students could advance their knowledge of various art subjects. The planet also featured a shipbuilding industry, using ore imported from the nearby planet [Kreeling](/wiki/Kreeling "Kreeling").[[48]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-48)

Both the Naboo and Gungans had a close relationship with water.[[12]](#cite_note-SWCL-12) [Fish](/wiki/Fish "Fish") was an important [food](/wiki/Foodstuff "Foodstuff") to the people of Naboo.[[48]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-48) Naboo had [engagement rituals](/wiki/Naboo_engagement_rituals "Naboo engagement rituals") during the [High Republic Era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era") intended to be performed between the betrothed individuals.[[94]](#cite_note-Adventures_7-94)

## Behind the scenes[]

Naboo first appeared in the [1999](/wiki/1999 "1999") film [*Star Wars*: Episode I *The Phantom Menace*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace "Star Wars: Episode I The Phantom Menace"), the first installment of the *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* [prequel trilogy](/wiki/Prequel_trilogy "Prequel trilogy").[[13]](#cite_note-TPM-13) It was later featured in [2002](/wiki/2002 "2002")'s [*Star Wars*: Episode II *Attack of the Clones*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones "Star Wars: Episode II Attack of the Clones")[[21]](#cite_note-AotC-21) and [2005](/wiki/2005 "2005")'s [*Star Wars*: Episode III *Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith").[[80]](#cite_note-Episode_III-80)

After many months of general research into where to shoot,[[95]](#cite_note-Ask-95) the real-world shooting locations for Naboo were [Villa del Balbianello](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Villa_del_Balbianello) and [Royal Palace of Caserta](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caserta_Palace "wikipedia:Caserta Palace") in [Italy](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italy "wikipedia:Italy") and [Plaza de España in Seville](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Plaza_de_Espa%C3%B1a,_Seville "wikipedia:Plaza de España, Seville"), [Spain](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spain "wikipedia:Spain"), among others. The buildings of Naboo were based on the [Hagia Sophia](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hagia_Sophia "wikipedia:Hagia Sophia"), a cathedral turned mosque then turned museum located in [Istanbul](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Istanbul "wikipedia:Istanbul"), [Turkey](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkey "wikipedia:Turkey"). On the other hand, the architecture of Naboo was inspired by the domed and scalloped roofs of the [Marin County Civic Center](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marin_County_Civic_Center "wikipedia:Marin County Civic Center").[[96]](#cite_note-Art_of_Solo-96) The crew hoped to depict Naboo with classical architecture, thereby establishing the planet's scale and giving the idea of a sophisticated society.[[95]](#cite_note-Ask-95)

The exact number of moons in Naboo is currently unknown. In *Attack of the Clones*, [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu") mentions "spice miners on the moons of Naboo."[[21]](#cite_note-AotC-21) However, the [2016](/wiki/2016 "2016") reference book [*Star Wars: Complete Locations*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Complete_Locations_(2016) "Star Wars: Complete Locations (2016)") states that Naboo has only one moon.[[12]](#cite_note-SWCL-12) The [2018](/wiki/2018 "2018") novel *[Thrawn: Alliances](/wiki/Thrawn:_Alliances "Thrawn: Alliances")* confirms that Naboo has three moons.[[9]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-9) There is also a discrepancy over the names of the three moons: *[Nexus of Power](/wiki/Nexus_of_Power "Nexus of Power")* states that the moons where [Ohma-D'un](/wiki/Ohma-D%27un "Ohma-D'un"), [Rori](/wiki/Rori "Rori"), and a small third moon that has no [in-universe](/wiki/In-universe "In-universe") name,[[16]](#cite_note-Nexus_of_Power-16) while *[Rise of the Separatists](/wiki/Rise_of_the_Separatists "Rise of the Separatists")*, a sourcebook from *[Star Wars Roleplaying](/wiki/Star_Wars_Roleplaying "Star Wars Roleplaying")*, states that the three moons of Naboo are [Rori](/wiki/Rori "Rori"), [Veruna](/wiki/Veruna "Veruna"), and [Ohma-D'un](/wiki/Ohma-D%27un "Ohma-D'un").[[7]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Separatists-7) However, the novel *[Leia, Princess of Alderaan](/wiki/Leia,_Princess_of_Alderaan "Leia, Princess of Alderaan")* prominently includes the moon [Onoam](/wiki/Onoam "Onoam").[[10]](#cite_note-Leia-10) Rori and Onoam have similar descriptions,[[10]](#cite_note-Leia-10)[[16]](#cite_note-Nexus_of_Power-16) but as yet there has been no clarification for the discrepancy.

[↑](#cite_ref-228_Date_68-0) *[The High Republic: Temptation of the Force](/wiki/The_High_Republic:_Temptation_of_the_Force "The High Republic: Temptation of the Force")* establishes that **Naboo** became part of the [Occlusion Zone](/wiki/Occlusion_Zone "Occlusion Zone") following the [Stormwall's first expansion](/wiki/Expansion_of_the_Stormwall "Expansion of the Stormwall") but before the events of the novel. [*The High Republic Adventures* (2023) 4](/wiki/The_High_Republic_Adventures_(2023)_4 "The High Republic Adventures (2023) 4") and *Temptation of the Force* commence one [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") and two [weeks](/wiki/Standard_week "Standard week") and one year and six weeks after the [Starlight Beacon's destruction](/wiki/Destruction_of_Starlight_Beacon "Destruction of Starlight Beacon"), respectively, dating both to [228 BBY](/wiki/228_BBY "228 BBY") per the reasoning [here](/wiki/Template:StarlightDate "Template:StarlightDate"). As [*The High Republic Adventures* (2023) 6](/wiki/The_High_Republic_Adventures_(2023)_6 "The High Republic Adventures (2023) 6")—which depicts the Stormwall's first expansion—takes place immediately following *The High Republic Adventures* (2023) 4, Naboo must have been brought into the Occlusion Zone in 228 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system"). As *Temptation of the Force* establishes that Naboo was conquered after it was brought into the Occlusion Zone, it must have occurred that year. 69. ↑ [69.0](#cite_ref-:0_69-0) [69.1](#cite_ref-:0_69-1) *[The High Republic: Temptation of the Force](/wiki/The_High_Republic:_Temptation_of_the_Force "The High Republic: Temptation of the Force")* 70. [↑](#cite_ref-132Date_70-0) [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") ["Lost/Found" Episode Guide | The Acolyte](https://www.starwars.com/series/the-acolyte/lost-found-episode-guide) on [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20240613105150/https://www.starwars.com/series/the-acolyte/lost-found-episode-guide)) states that the events of *[Star Wars: The Acolyte](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Acolyte "Star Wars: The Acolyte")* take place 100 [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the events of [*Star Wars*: Episode I *The Phantom Menace*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace "Star Wars: Episode I The Phantom Menace"), which *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates to [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY"). Therefore, *The Acolyte* takes place in [132 BBY](/wiki/132_BBY "132 BBY"). 71. [↑](#cite_ref-Date_92-0) *[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker:_The_Visual_Dictionary "Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary")* dates the events of *Star Wars*: Episode IX *The Rise of Skywalker* as taking place one [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") after the "[Starkiller Incident](/wiki/Hosnian_Cataclysm "Hosnian Cataclysm")." As *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* dates the Starkiller Incident to [34 ABY](/wiki/34_ABY "34 ABY"), it can be deduced the events of *Star Wars*: Episode IX *The Rise of Skywalker* take place in 35 [ABY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system"). 93. [↑](#cite_ref-TROS_Junior_Novel_93-0) *[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: A Junior Novel](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker:_A_Junior_Novel "Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: A Junior Novel")* 94.
